<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:scharrel.html>scharrel</a> (24394)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scharrel.html>scharrel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scharrel.html>scharrels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scharrel.html>scharreltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">action<span class="ib-comma">,</span> especially in "<a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:scharrel.html>scharrel</a>"</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> picking up, seeking a casual sex partner.</li>
<li>fuckmate, person with whom one <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an irregular, noncommittal, superficial love relationship.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The grammatical gender of this word does not depend on the biological gender of the person referred to.

<p>Frequentative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">scharren</i> (now archaic).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to mess around, to potter</li>
<li>to piece together, to gather from scattered <a href = vnd.unilang:bits.html>bits</a> and pieces</li></ol>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schat.html>schat</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">treasure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kist.html>kist</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schat.html>schat</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">darling; treasure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bout</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sweetheart, dear; haunch, prized meat-cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schedel.html>schedel</a> (3601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schedele</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">skēthila</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*skeithila</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">part, crown, crest, summit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skaidilō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">part in the hair, top, crown, crest, summit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*SkÁit-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut, part, separate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Scheitel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">part, crest, apex</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***scheef.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:scheef.html>scheef</a> (11294)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">scheyff</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skaibaz</i> ‘crooked, askew’, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*skeh₂iwo-</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scaevus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">left, clumsy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σκαιός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skaiós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rude; brusque</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">šķìbs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crooked</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Cognate with German (obsolete) <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">scheif</i>, (dialectal) <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">scheib</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">*sc(e)āf</i> (in <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">scāffōt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">splay-footed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">skev</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheef.html>scheef</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheef.html>schever</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">scheefst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>crooked, not level or straight
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuin.html>schuin</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> weird, not right</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">scēve</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skibō-</i>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Schääv</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schäbe</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shive</i>, all ‘fragment of the <a href = vnd.unilang:woody.html>woody</a> core of flax or hemp’.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheef.html>scheef</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheef.html>scheven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheef.html>scheefje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">textiles</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shive, i.e. fragment of the <a href = vnd.unilang:woody.html>woody</a> core of flax or hemp
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leem.html>leem</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:scheef.html>scheef</a></b>
</p>

***scheel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:scheel.html>scheel</a> (20234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">scelu</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">scele</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*skelo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skelhaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)kel-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lean, bend; joint</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheel.html>scheel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">sceolh</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">skjalgr</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scelus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crime</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σκολιός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skoliós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σκαληνός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skalēnós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheel.html>scheel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheel.html>scheler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">scheelst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cross-eyed, squinting</li>
<li>crooked, <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a>, not straight</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative sense</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> with an envious or jealous look</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a pain or painful issue</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> severe</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sour, <a href = vnd.unilang:tart.html>tart</a></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schijnen.html>schene</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*skina</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skinō</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schiene</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shin</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:scheenbeen.html>scheenbeen</a> (33846)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheen.html>scheen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schienbein</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shinbone</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">skinneben</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">skenben</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheenbeen.html>scheenbeen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheenbenen.html>scheenbenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheenbeen.html>scheenbeentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:tibia.html>tibia</a> (bone of the <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a>).</li>
<li>A shin, the front of a vertebrate <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a> beneath the knee.</li></ol>

***scheiding.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:scheiding.html>scheiding</a> (2908)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheiden.html>scheiden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>. Cognate to English shedding.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheiding.html>scheiding</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheidingen.html>scheidingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheidinkje.html>scheidinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>(<i>between <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a></i>) <span class="Latn" lang="en">separation</span></li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">divorce</span>.
<ul><li><b>1992</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A._F._Th._van_der_Heijden" class="extiw" title="w:A. F. Th. van der Heijden">A. F. Th. <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Heijden</a>, <i>Weerborstels</i>, Em. Querido's <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgeverij.html>Uitgeverij</a>, page 36:
<dl><dd>'<a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a> in <b><a href = vnd.unilang:scheiding.html>scheiding</a></b>,' <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorde.html>hoorde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geregeld.html>geregeld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fluisteren.html>fluisteren</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:familie.html>familie</a>.
<dl><dd>'They are in the process of <b>divorce</b> ', I often <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> family members whisper.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A parting, a part <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">hairstyle</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">divorce</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:echtscheiding.html>echtscheiding</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***scheids.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:scheids.html>scheids</a> (11847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Clipping of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheidsrechter.html>scheidsrechter</a></i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheiden.html>scheiden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to separate, to decide, to referee</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">genitive interfix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***scheien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:scheien.html>scheien</a> (100140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">skiuhen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skiuhwijaną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">scheuen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuwen.html>schuwen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">eschew</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shy</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheien.html>scheien</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular present</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheit.html>scheit</a></b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb">gescheit</b>, <i>auxiliary verb</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb">hunn</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to eschew, to shun, to shy away from</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shy</li></ol>

***schelden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schelden.html>schelden</a> (9589)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schelden.html>schelden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">skeldan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skeldaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schelden.html>schelden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to scold, to swear</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheldpartij.html>scheldpartij</a></span></li>

***schelvis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schelvis.html>schelvis</a> (73041)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schelvisch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">scelvisc</i>. Analyzable as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schel.html>schel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">peel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vis.html>vis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the former being a dated variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schil.html>schil</a></i>. The name <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due either to the relatively large scales or to the layered meat of the fish. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schellfisch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***schenken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schenken.html>schenken</a> (5258)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schenken.html>schenken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">skenken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skankijaną</i>. The verb, which originally <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> weak, became strong in the early modern period by analogy with related class 3 strong verbs such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drinken.html>drinken</a></i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shink</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">skink</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pour, give as a present</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to give as a present, to gift

***schennis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schennis.html>schennis</a> (100132)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schennisse</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schendenisse</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schenden.html>schenden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to violate, damage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schennis.html>schennis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schennis.html>schennissen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An active or passive case of hurting, damaging</li>
<li>An immoral violation of a person, obligation or rule</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A result of the above: shame, dishonor, scandal</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The potential to hurt or damage: danger, risk</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***scheppen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:scheppen.html>scheppen</a> (4297)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheppen.html>scheppen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*skeppen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skapjaną</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shape</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheppen.html>scheppen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to create
<ul><li><b>1637</b>, Statenvertaling, Genesis 1,1.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">In den <a href = vnd.unilang:beginne.html>beginne</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:schiep.html>schiep</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hemel.html>hemel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">In the beginning, <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> <b>made</b> the heaven and the earth.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schep.html>schep</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheppen.html>scheppen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scoop (up), to shovel (away)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hit and subsequently heave up (by a vehicle at high speed)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:getuigen.html>Getuigen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meldden.html>meldden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> één <a href = vnd.unilang:voertuig.html>voertuig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:geschept.html>geschept</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voertuigen.html>voertuigen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geraakt.html>geraakt</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>Witnesses reported that the woman <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> shovelled up in the air by one car and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> then hit by two other cars.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>root of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheppen.html>scheppen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to create</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>

***schepsel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schepsel.html>schepsel</a> (8633)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>from the root of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheppen.html>scheppen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to create</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-sel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">which indicates a result</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schepsel.html>schepsel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schepsels.html>schepsels</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schepselen.html>schepselen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schepseltje.html>schepseltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>creature, a life form (believed to be created in most religious traditions)</li>
<li>wretch; vulnerable, contemptible, or miserable individual</li></ol>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:creatuur.html>creatuur</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemaakt.html>gemaakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:scheren.html>scheren</a> (4652)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schēren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">skeran</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skeraną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)ker-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheren.html>scheren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shave (reflexive pronouns are used for self-directed actions)

***scherp.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:scherp.html>scherp</a> (2715)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">scharp</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:scherp.html>scherp</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">skarp</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skarpaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scherp.html>scherp</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scherper.html>scherper</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scherpst.html>scherpst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sharp, able to cut easily</li>
<li>alert, on the ball</li>
<li>clever, intelligent, witty</li>
<li>acute, having a small angle</li>
<li>in focus, clearly visible, not blurry</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of food</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hot, spicy</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scherp.html>scherp</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scherpen.html>scherpen</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scherpen.html>scherpen</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:scherp.html>scherp</a></b>
